Matters discussed: (1) Resolved to promulgate the personnel lawsuit procedure of Chapter 4, Part 5 of the Civil Procedure Law; (2) Resolved to promulgate the Anti-Dumping Duty Law; (3) Resolved to promulgate the Factory Inspection Law; (4) Resolved to promulgate the Regulations and Repayment Schedule for the Hubei Province Post-Disaster Public Bonds of the 20th Year of the Republic of China; (5) Resolved that before the establishment of the Directorate-General of Budget, all matters stipulated in the Directorate-General of Budget Organization Law should be handled by the Directorate-General of Budget Preparatory Office first, and the head of the Preparatory Office should draft and submit the necessary personnel, expenses, and procedures for approval, and issue a circular to all agencies inside and outside the capital to follow the Supplementary Measures for the Trial Budget Regulations of the 19th Year and send the 20th Year budget to the Directorate-General of Budget Preparatory Office for review and compilation; (6) Resolved to specially appoint Sun Ke as Deputy Director of the National Assembly Election Office; (7) Resolved that: 1. The Huai River Commission should be reorganized immediately based on the amended organization law. 2. Chiang Kai-shek is specially appointed as Chairman, Huang Fu as Vice Chairman, and Zhuang Songfu, Chen Qicai, Chen Lifu, Wu Zhongxin, Yang Yongtai, Zhang Renjie, Wu Jingheng, Chen Huide, Duan Xipeng, Li Yizhi, Shen Baixian, Wang Zhen, Xu Shiying, Chen Maojie, Tu Qi, Shen Yi, and Chen Yi as commissioners, and Zhuang Songfu, Chen Qicai, Chen Lifu, Wu Zhongxin, and Yang Yongtai are designated as Standing Commissioners. 3. Before Vice Chairman Huang Fu assumes office, Standing Commissioner Zhuang Songfu is specially appointed to act as his agent. 4. Shen Baixian is appointed concurrently as Director of the Secretariat. 5. Starting from January of this year, the Ministry of Finance will allocate a monthly operating fund of 30,000 yuan; (8) Resolved to appoint Chen Zhuoru as Chief of Staff of the Jiangsu Pacification Superintendent's Office and Yu Dianshu as Chief of the Staff Office of the Jiangsu Pacification Superintendent's Office; (9) Premier Chiang, concurrently the President of the Executive Yuan, submitted a report from the Ministry of Education that the Beiyang Institute of Technology reported that the American metallurgy professor Shi Boli will have completed 20 years of service at the school by July of this year, and at the age of 74, his eyesight and hearing are gradually failing, and he intends to retire during the summer vacation of this year and requested that a pension be issued. The report was forwarded for review and approval. Resolved to approve the payment of a pension.

Jin Sui Generals' Recent Meeting 76

▲ Three Measures Decided

Taiyuan Dispatch: The issue of military streamlining in Jin Province has gradually become smooth after recent mediation by various parties. However, small group meetings of various factions are still held from time to time. Xu, Yang, and others originally scheduled a formal meeting at the headquarters the day before yesterday (30th), but it was adjourned after only a few people discussed it for a long time because the military commanders were not all present. Yesterday afternoon, at about 3 p.m., a final formal agreement was made in the Senate Hall of the headquarters. The following is a description of the process: Before the meeting of the Jin Sui generals in the Senate Hall, Zeng Zhi, Gao Buqing, Zhang Hanjie, and Fu Cunhuai explained everything to the military commanders. The military commanders then had a detailed discussion and exchanged opinions at Zhang Huizhao's private residence at No. 26, Zhengjie Street, Xinmin, at 12:00 noon. At 3:00 p.m., Yang Aiyuan, Feng Pengzhu, Wang Jingguo, Li Fuying, Yang Yaofang, Yang Xiaou, Zhang Huizhao, Sun Chu, Yang Chengyuan, Li Shengda, and the cavalry commander Zhao Chengzhou, the military police commander Li Runfa, the artillery commander Zhou Dai, and the mediators Zhang Hanjie, Gao Buqing, Fu Cunhuai, and Chen Zengzhi all arrived. At 3:30, Xu Yongchang and Shang Zhen continued to attend the meeting, and the meeting was declared open. First, the mediator explained the opinions of the generals and the mediator's proposals, and then the discussion began. Xu Yongchang, Sun Chu, Wang Jingguo, Feng Pengzhu and others spoke one after another. At 4:30, the four mediators, Chen Zengzhi and others, withdrew, and the generals continued to discuss. The newly appointed military commanders Shang, Xu, and Yang all expressed their willingness to give up their positions as military commanders. In other words, the military commander system will not be established. The results are as follows: (1) The organization will still be eight divisions, and the division commanders will be Wang Jingguo, Feng Pengzhu, Yang Yaofang, Yang Xiaou, Li Shengda, Yang Chengyuan, and Fu Zuoyi. As for Sun Chu's army, it will be reorganized into a railway protection army. The vacant position of division commander will be filled by Li Fuying or Zhang Huizhao. (2) Three garrison commands will be established in southern Jin, northern Jin, and Taiyuan, and will be filled by Rong Honglu, Zhang Huizhao, and Li Fuying. Each garrison command will be in charge of two regiments of the army. (3) The original main commanders of the military commanders retained 60 regiments. Now Zhang of Liaoning has agreed to establish 50 large regiments. According to these 50 large regiments, the number is even greater than that of 60 regiments, so this problem can also be solved. (4) The Military Commission discussed for an hour. Because the opinions of the generals on the candidates were not consistent, no decision was made. Finally, it was agreed to send representatives to Liaoning to ask Vice Commander Zhang for instructions on everything within days. The meeting adjourned at 7:50 p.m. (February 2nd)

Jin People's Two Major Demands Recently 77

▲Consolidating Provincial Currency ▲Taking over and Reforming the Arsenal

Taiyuan Dispatch: Since Yan's retirement and the great changes in Jin Province, the people of Jin have originally had three major demands for the aftermath of the Jin situation. The first is the issue of the provincial chairman, which is related to the safety of the entire province. It is advocated that Jin people govern Jin. The second is the issue of the provincial currency, which is related to the people's livelihood in the entire province. It is advocated to earnestly request the central government to restore the originally planned public debt of 24 million yuan to consolidate Shanxi's finances, or to find ways to cash it out quickly in the province. The third is the arsenal that sucks the people's blood and sweat. It is advocated to return it to the people and transform it into a production agency. When Yan first left, the selection of the provincial chairman was the most intense. Some advocated Kong Xiangxi, some advocated Wen Shouquan, and some advocated Sun Chu. Discussions were held either outside the province or within the province. The discussions were mixed and endless. After the Tianjin Agreement was reached and the central government issued the order to appoint Shang Zhen, although the voice of military and civilian separation was still being chanted loudly, there was not much mention of the slogan of Jin people governing Jin. Today, what the people of Jin Province urgently need is to consolidate the provincial currency and reorganize the arsenal. These two are interrelated, and the people feel the pain most deeply. This demand has recently been specifically put forward by the two major people's organizations, the Provincial Party Department and the Post-Disaster Reconstruction Promotion Association, and listed as the two major central movements of the people. Regarding the issue of consolidating the provincial currency, in addition to unanimously requesting the central government to issue financial public bonds, the Party Department has recently been actively carrying out the process of requesting the provincial government to implement the liquidation of Yan's assets to offset the 6 million yuan in cash that Yan had withdrawn from the provincial government before his departure. The provincial government is responsible for recovering it. However, whether it can be done in practice is doubtful. After all, the number of Yan's movable properties is unknown to those who are not insiders. Before Yan left, the soft furnishings used in the headquarters' private residence were all transported back to his original hometown by car. Since the person has left, how could he be willing to leave his savings in Jin? Moreover, it is certain that Yan has deposited money in foreign banks for several years, so it is naturally not easy to liquidate the movable properties. As for his immovable properties, there are very few. It is said that the value of Yan's ancestral land and houses is less than 10,000 yuan. As for those in Bingyuan, there are only two residences in Donghuayuan and Xihuayuan, one residence in Tongshun Lane, the old Jin Sheng Bank and Jin Yu Grain Store, the Daoshengheng Pharmacy and other shop addresses, and a small number of shares in various commercial firms. Even if all of them are searched, I am afraid it will not be more than 300,000 yuan. I don't know how the provincial government will start. In order to respond to the demands of the people, the provincial government has decided to implement a monthly lottery of 500,000 yuan in cash in the near future. However, this is just a kind of decoration in the depreciation of banknotes. No one has mentioned the fundamental solution. As for the issue of transforming the arsenal into a livelihood agency, it is most justified in terms of reason and logic. However, the nature of an arsenal is different from that of an ordinary factory, and whether the environment will allow it is still a problem. In addition to expanding publicity and carrying out various activities, the Party Department and various associations have specifically telegraphed the central government yesterday to formally request it. The text is as follows: To the Central Executive Committee of the Kuomintang in Nanjing: We have submitted proposals regarding the aftermath of Shanxi. We should briefly state the method of handling the Shanxi arsenal. We have not yet received a reply. I am very anxious. I believe that this factory is deeply and greatly related to the safety of the party and the country and the happiness and misfortune of the people of Jin. I dare to express my humble opinion and list the outlines. The manufacture of munitions in this factory is nothing less than a talisman for warlords and a fuse for civil wars. It is actually a tool for slaughtering the people. Last year, Yan rebelled and dared to betray the central government. The weapons he relied on were the most important part of this factory. The people of Jin are determined to learn from the past and prevent future troubles. They all believe that this factory should not exist. If we do not take this opportunity to resolutely eliminate it, one day it will fall into the hands of ambitious people and be controlled by one person or one faction. I am afraid that it will have the resources to create chaos and that supervision will be difficult. If the situation is stirred up, it will be enough to use it to poison the people and bring disaster to the local area. This is the first reason why this factory should be resolved as soon as possible. This factory was originally formed by Yan sucking the essence of the people of Jin and squeezing the people's fat. It has been operating for more than ten years and has cost tens of millions of dollars. Now, in order to prevent turmoil and develop industry, we should use the original foundation of this factory to establish a large-scale production agency, so that the blood capital that the people of Jin have paid for more than ten years will still be returned to the public of all the people of Jin for the purpose of producing food and clothing. All the workers in the factory can also maintain their livelihoods, so that they will not be displaced and become bandits. In a single transition, all the benefits will be available. This is the second reason why this factory should be resolved as soon as possible. If the central government believes that it is necessary to continue to maintain the factory for national defense, it should also prevent problems before they occur and not repeat the mistakes of the past. It should quickly send personnel to inspect and accept it, estimate a reasonable price, and compensate all the people of Jin, so as to relieve the financial crisis and handle all the aftermath matters. At the same time, the factory should be taken over by the central government for direct jurisdiction, so as to avoid the powerful seizing the opportunity to occupy it, causing the local people to suffer from war again. This is the third reason why this factory should be resolved as soon as possible. The above-mentioned reasons and methods are considered by our association to be of the utmost importance to the lives and property of all the people of Jin. We should telegraph this to your association for review and approval, and then request the National Government to adopt and implement it. We are looking forward to your order. Shanxi Provincial Executive Committee of the Kuomintang (February 1st)

Joint Suppression of Bandits Between Anhui, Jiangsu, and Henan 78

Bengbu Dispatch: The border area between Anhui, Jiangsu, and Henan provinces has become a zone where bandits run rampant due to the impact of years of war. Therefore, bandits are everywhere in Su County, Xiao County, Yongcheng, and Xiayi counties, and looting occurs almost every day. Moreover, the mountains and ridges are mixed, making it particularly difficult to suppress them. Moreover, defeated soldiers and vagrants are mixed with them, and the residents suffer unspeakable devastation. In November last year, the Lin Huan and Bai Shan areas in the northwest of Su County were disturbed by the defeated soldiers of Sun Dianying's army. They were dispersed by the troops and militias of Su and Yong counties. However, the accumulated bandits in the northwest have been entrenched for a long time and have not been eliminated. Recently, more than 2,000 defeated soldiers, led by Yang Xiyue, have come to Nanpiqiaoji (territory of Yongcheng), which is more than 70 miles northwest of Suixi County. They are armed with artillery, machine guns, and mortars, and occupy more than 40 villages, killing, looting, and plundering, no different from bandits. The Yongcheng garrison reported the news and sent a regiment to suppress them. Because of the weak force, more than 100 soldiers were injured by the defeated soldiers. Now they are increasing the deployment of troops to block the south of the county. As for Xiayi in eastern Henan, more than 100 defeated soldiers have recently joined forces with Wang Liuni, a bandit in Xiao County, with more than 200 men, and窜 to Zhuxiaozhuang, which is at the junction of Su, Yong, and Xiao counties, and a part of them have occupied Zhangji in the Suixi area. The area immediately mobilized the People's Self-Defense Corps to block them. In addition, the bandit atmosphere in the area of Xiangli in the northern part of Su County has also been fierce recently. Hualou, which is about two miles north of Caili, has been occupied by bandits. The remaining 200 bandits who overturned officials have also joined the Hualou bandits and are preparing to confront the government army. The Suixi People's Self-Defense Corps and the First Battalion of the Su County Police Reserve Regiment recently stationed in Tuxingwei, and notified the Second Battalion of the Police Reserve Regiment stationed in Nanjieting and the Xiao County Police Regiment stationed in Xiaoshicun to jointly attack the bandits in Hualou, and searched for the accumulated bandits in Shantao Songzhuang area. They are currently under siege. (January 4th)

Financial Difficulties in Jiangxi Province 80

▲New Measures for Addressing Both Immediate and Underlying Problems Formulated by the Provincial Government

Nanchang Dispatch: Jiangxi's bandit-stricken areas are vast. Of the province's 81 counties, only a dozen or so can remit funds. Revenue is less than 20-30% of the budget. When Chen Jiadong was the director of the Department of Finance, he already felt that all resources were exhausted. After Huang Bozhong took over, the monthly budget of 1.2 million local revenue was only 70,000-80,000 yuan. Therefore, in addition to borrowing shop rents for three months in the provincial capital, borrowing funds from merchants with beneficial circulating coupons, and issuing tens of thousands of yuan of short-term treasury bonds to be used as rice rations for the bandit suppression troops, administrative expenses were in arrears for three to four months, education expenses were in arrears for five to six months, treasury bonds fell to 20-30% of their face value, and circulating coupons were only worth 70-80% of their face value. After the elimination of the likin, the annual shortage was 1.7-1.8 million yuan. The future of finance is unimaginable. However, the province is once again full of troops, and military spending is particularly urgent. Therefore, the provincial government is paying close attention to this. In addition to requesting the central government to bear all the expenses for bandit suppression, it has also formulated measures to address the immediate problems: (1) The Department of Finance will send personnel to various counties near the provincial capital that have not been affected by bandits to urge the collection of grain tribute; (2) Director Huang of the Department of Finance will persuade the business community in the province to sell 200,000 yuan of treasury bonds to solve the urgent problem. The underlying problems were also addressed: 1. Request the central government to return the 3 million yuan advanced by the provincial treasury; 2. Telegraph Beijing to request that after the salt surcharge tax is turned over to the central government, the education, treasury bond, and circulating coupon funds will still be borne by the salt tax and salt surcharge tax, or that public bonds will be allocated to repay them; 3. All livestock tax will be returned to the Ministry of Finance for its own management. All subsidies for the two eliminations of the likin will be paid by the Ministry of Finance from the salt tax; 4. Various post-war reconstruction expenses in the province will be allowed to be offset by the land tax, and post-war reconstruction bonds will be issued (the amount is undetermined); 5. The budget for the 19th year will absolutely adhere to the policy of austerity; 6. Business tax will be implemented. The Department of Finance will formulate detailed rules in accordance with the business tax regulations promulgated by the central government to facilitate implementation. In addition, the municipal finance bureau is also preparing to conduct business registration to facilitate tax collection and increase revenue. (January 31st)

Guangdong Province Imposes Three Unified Taxes 81

▲New Regulations on Tax Rates for Cotton Yarn, Matches, and Cement

▲Cigarette Tax Also Imposed on February 1st

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the elimination of the likin in Guangdong, various special taxes have been imposed to offset the loss of the likin tax. The unified taxes on cotton yarn, matches, and cement have been levied since February 1st. The Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian Unified Tax Bureau has formulated tax rates for these three items respectively. After that day, all domestically produced and imported cotton yarn, matches, and cement must be reported and inspected at the local management office, inspection office, branch office, or factory representative before they can be sold. The tax rates for these three unified taxes are as follows: (1) Cotton yarn: 2.75 yuan per 100 catties for those within 23 strands, 3.75 yuan for those exceeding that, and 5% of the price for others; (2) Matches: 5 yuan per large box for those less than 43 mm in length or less than 75 sticks per box, 7.5 yuan for those 52 mm in length or less than 100 sticks, and 10 yuan for those exceeding that. Each large box contains 7,200 boxes; (3) Cement: 6 jiao per barrel weighing 380 pounds. If it exceeds or falls short of this, the tax will be levied proportionally. In addition to import duties, imported goods will still be subject to the unified tax. Domestically produced goods are exempt from export tax. In addition, taxes on cigarettes, cigars, etc. will also be increased at the same time. The tax rates have been set by the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian Unified Tax Bureau and will be implemented on the 1st according to the new unified tax rates. The tax rates are as follows: A. Cigarettes: (1) The registered price is more than 545 yuan, which is the first class. The previous unified tax was 225 yuan, and the new regulations now set the tax at 305 yuan in national currency; (2) The price is more than 150 yuan to 540 yuan, which is the second class. The previous tax was 56 yuan, and the new tax is 81 yuan; (3) The price is less than 150 yuan, which is the third class. The previous tax was 32 yuan, and the new tax is 39 yuan. B. Cigars: (1) The price is more than 60 yuan, and those without trademarks are the first class. The previous tax was 29.25 yuan, and the new tax is 45 yuan; (2) The price is more than 30 yuan and less than 60 yuan, which is the second class. The previous tax was 12.675 yuan, and the new tax is 22.5 yuan; (3) The price is more than 15 yuan and less than 30 yuan, which is the third class. The previous tax was 7.313 yuan, and the new tax is 11.25 yuan; (4) The price is more than 7.5 yuan and less than 15 yuan, which is the fourth class. The previous tax was 3.656 yuan, and the new tax is 5.65 yuan; (5) The price is more than 4.5 yuan and less than 7.5 yuan, which is the fifth class. The previous tax was 1.950 yuan, and the new tax is 3 yuan; (6) The price is less than 4.5 yuan, which is the sixth class. The previous tax was 1.463 yuan, and the new tax is 2.25 yuan. The above-mentioned grades and classes, if the old tax stamps have been affixed and the goods have left the factory or been imported before January 31, should be allowed to be sold without paying additional tax. The new tax rates will be implemented uniformly on February 1.

County Magistrate Chen immediately ordered him to be suspended and appointed Huang Zhenmin, a trainee at the district chief training center, to act as the district chief.

Suzhou 85

A Sailing Ship Was Robbed in Donghui Port. A sailing ship traveling between Suzhou and Changshu was suddenly encountered by a bandit ship with five or six bandits speaking the Chaohu dialect in Donghui Port, Sheshan, Taihu Lake the day before (4th). More than 400 yuan of foreign currency and 140 yuan of Hongyuan Zhuang's promissory notes and 100 yuan of Yongsheng Zhuang's promissory notes were robbed. The shipowner, A San, came to the city yesterday (6th) to report to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

The Reporters Association Was Reorganized into a Joint Association. The Suzhou News Reporters Association has been reorganized into the Wuxian News Reporters Joint Association. Preparatory members have been nominated and the County Party Department has approved the convening of a preparatory meeting on the afternoon of the 6th. The meeting resolved: (1) To appoint Li Tianxuan, Yan Gaisheng, and Wang Weigong to draft the articles of association; (2) To register members immediately, and complete the registration within one week; (3) To formulate an outline for member registration.

A Shopping Mall Was Built on the Shadow Wall of Xuanmiao Temple. The construction company built a shopping mall at the site of the Shadow Wall of Xuanmiao Temple. The National Goods Relief Association had submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for approval. The site is a scenic spot with historical sites, and people from China and foreign countries are concerned about it. If stores are opened, they are limited to selling national goods and are not allowed to sell foreign goods. The county government was ordered to comply. The county government has now approved the request of Abbot Yan Juecang and merchants such as Xiang Xunru and others after they submitted a detailed report and signed a land lease contract, started building houses, and have no stores specializing in foreign goods, which also implies the intention to promote national goods. The county government has approved the request. At the shareholder meeting held by the National Goods Relief Association on the 6th, some people, including Bu Gengxin, proposed that since someone had submitted a request to the county government for approval, the tone of the request was that there were no stores specializing in foreign goods, which also implied the intention to promote national goods. It was obvious that the intention was to also sell foreign goods, which violated the orders of the Executive Yuan. The meeting resolved to submit a request to the county government to strictly enforce the orders of the Executive Yuan, and to issue a notice ordering the stores in the area to absolutely not sell foreign goods in order to comply with the orders of the Executive Yuan and maintain national goods.

The Battalion Commander's Counter-Revolution Case Was Pardoned and Released. Zhang Baohua, the battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the 148th Regiment of the 74th Brigade of the Army, who was formerly stationed in Yancheng County, was falsely accused of counter-revolution and murder. The case was transferred to the High Court for trial. Last month, the court ruled that he was not guilty of murder and pardoned him for counter-revolution. He was immediately returned to the Third Branch Prison. Now that the prosecutor's appeal period has passed, the Criminal Court proposed his release at 2 pm yesterday. Zhang 詧 Requested the Return of Property. Zhang 詧, a gentry from Nantong County, was accused of colluding with the enemy when the National Revolutionary Army conquered Jiangsu. The Jiangsu Provincial Government was ordered to confiscate Zhang's property. Several years have passed. Now that the National Government has promulgated an amnesty decree for political prisoners, Zhang 詧 recently submitted a petition to the High Court, stating the reasons for the false accusation of collusion with the enemy and the confiscation of property, and requesting the application of the amnesty decree and the return of his property. After receiving the petition, the High Court ruled that Zhang 詧's request was not in compliance with the procedures and should be submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government. The ruling was issued yesterday (6th). Bandits From Wu Port Arrived at Daguhu 　Wu, a place in Wujiang County, at the junction of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, was 窜 to by more than 200 bandits from Changxing, Zhejiang Province, yesterday morning. They were fully armed and harassed merchants. After receiving a report, Xu Boying, the captain of the 14th Wujiang Water Police Team, immediately gathered the team's ships and led them to suppress the bandits at about 6 pm yesterday. In addition, dozens of bandits from Henan arrived near Zhouzhuang with the intention of robbing merchants and farmers. They were suppressed by the water and land police teams stationed in Fan. The bandits dispersed.

Wuxi 86

The Chamber of Commerce Convened a General Meeting of All Industries: The County Chamber of Commerce recently received repeated complaints from various industries stating that the newly drafted "Regulations on the Collection of Business Tax in Jiangsu Province" and its detailed implementation rules exceeded the Ministry's outline by nearly ten times. Furthermore, the daily inspections of stamp tax were causing disturbances everywhere. They requested a meeting to discuss countermeasures. Therefore, on the afternoon of the 5th, a general meeting of representatives from various industries was convened, attended by 74 people from 43 industries. Chen Zhanru presided over the meeting, and the following resolutions were made: (A) Regarding the business tax issue, the chairman first reported that the recently promulgated Outline for the Collection of Business Tax by the Ministry and the nine articles of the outline decided at the 17th Reorganization Conference differed significantly in content. The chamber had already telegraphed the Ministry requesting an explanation and planned to jointly discuss countermeasures with the chambers of commerce of various counties in the shortest possible time. After discussion, it was decided (1) to appoint Qian Sunqing and Cheng Jing堂 as representatives to attend the joint meeting of chambers of commerce of various counties; (2) each industry should first submit written opinions to the chamber, which would then be handed over to the two representatives, Qian and Cheng, for reference. (B) Regarding the stamp tax issue, the chairman first reported on the recent request from the bureau for an increase in the assessed amount and the situation of inspectors checking outside. Then, the representative of the clothing industry reported that in the second-hand clothing store opened by Cheng Ziquan, the head of the stamp tax bureau's inspection team, the stamps on the account books were completely untaxed. He had obtained three copies of these books and asked if stamp tax bureau officials' account books in their stores were exempt from stamp tax. This immediately aroused strong emotions. As a result, it was decided (1) that the bureau should unconditionally return all checked account books to the shops; (2) to accommodate the bureau's opinion and increase the amount in accordance with the old quota as appropriate; (3) during the accounting period of the business community, the bureau shall not send inspectors to harass them again; (4) the three unstamped account books obtained by the clothing industry from Cheng Ziquan should be sent to the chamber for safekeeping pending further action.

Silk Factories Discuss Exemption from Special Silk Cocoon Tax: The Wuxi Silk Factory Association previously telegraphed the Ministry and Provincial authorities successively, requesting that the special tax on silk cocoons be exempted and that the silk factory industry be removed from category A, item 12 of the Jiangsu Province business tax rate table, which taxes silk factories at a rate of 10 per mille because the Ministry of Finance planned to levy a special tax on silk cocoons and silk exports constituted the bulk of foreign trade, the government should encourage it and not increase the levy. So far, no approval has been received. Recently, the Shanghai Silk Factory Association sent a letter discussing the reduction and exemption of the special tax and its position on business tax. Because this matter was of great importance, a meeting of all members was specially convened yesterday, chaired by Qian Fenghao. After merging and discussing the above cases, it was decided to continue to telegraph the Ministry and Provincial authorities in accordance with the previous resolution, requesting exemption from the special tax on silk cocoons and stating that the business tax was even more unacceptable.

Two Robberies in One Night in Rural Areas: Since winter, robbery cases have been frequent in the four rural districts of Xiyi. Although the authorities have ordered investigations and arrests, the number of cases solved remains very few. The night before last, two robberies occurred simultaneously in Taibo north of the two markets (cities): (1) At the intersection of Tu 141 and 342 of Gu池 Bridge, Taibo Market, District 12, on the direct road to Wangting D塘 River, at 12 o'clock the night before last, suddenly

A Robbery Occurred in Nancangwan in the City: Qu Guisheng, a resident of Nancangwan in the city, was known for his Yang style calligraphy. He has now resigned from his job. He frightened Ms. Lu into silence, tied up the gold earrings she wore and the scattered clothing in the room into two packages, and searched before leaving.

The First District Party Department Opposes the Demolition of Yuecheng: The First District Party Reorganization Committee held a regular meeting yesterday, chaired by Wu Luxiang. However, the Construction Bureau has bid to demolish the four city walls, including Yuecheng. It was decided to present this to the County Reorganization Committee to forward to the County Government to stop it in order to emphasize national defense. (2) Members of the Chamber of Commerce Standing Committee resigned one after another. The Truth of the Si圩 Robbery Case Investigated: The First Public Security Sub-bureau of Beiwai reported that a robbery had occurred at the home of Guang Feng in Si圩里, Hexi, and the Main Bureau has confirmed that it was Zhou Changgui, the deputy squad leader of Squad 8 of the Third Police Team, and police officers Liu Changsheng, Zhang Dengke, Meng Zhaoquan, Shan Jinlin, and Tang Rongsheng and Peng Yinchun, patrols of the Xicheng Police Station, who were searching for gambling and mistakenly reported it as a robbery case. Because Zhou Changgui had searched the people's residences without the order of his superiors, he was immediately detained and awaited interrogation and verification of the township chiefs, etc.

Hu Xiren Rescued from Danger: Hu Xiren, the friend of Hu Shoumin, the Education Committee member of the San官仓 Lin Bridge West District, was kidnapped by bandits the day before yesterday and forced to pay 7,000 yuan. The Li Hongze Case Concludes: Li Hongze, a former inspector of the Public Security Bureau, was involved in a fraud case with Xu Yun, Xu Yunliang, Li Rongbao, etc., in July of last year. Prison Break Occurs: The County Prison is crowded with prisoners. Last month, the bandit Xie Peizhi initiated a prison break, but it was fortunately reported by a fellow prisoner, Zhou Dianying, which prevented the attempt. Yesterday (5th) at about 1 p.m., Wang Jinbiao, a convicted drug trafficker from the north cell (sentenced to one year in prison, apprehended last year for escaping from prison, with an additional two years added), took advantage of the rainy and snowy weather to dig a small hole in the wall of the north cell. The hole was the original hole dug by Zhu Awu and others when they escaped from prison in February of last year. Chen Ada, an unconvicted thief, escaped. Zhenjiang 90

The Jiangsu Agricultural Department Promotes Fish Farming Cooperation: The Jiangsu Agricultural Department believes that Jiangsu Province has extremely rich natural aquatic products. However, because local areas lack improvement methods and sound organizations, the production volume cannot be fully increased. In order to develop the economy of ordinary people and promote aquaculture, the department has specially formulated model regulations for limited liability fish farming cooperatives and distributed them to various counties for reference.

Representatives of Pawnshops Came to the Province to Petition: The pawnshops of various counties in Jiangsu Province stated that Article 16 of the new regulations on pawnshops issued by the Construction Department stipulated that for monthly interest, every five days overdue would be calculated as half a month, and every fifteen days overdue would be calculated as one month. This was a significant difference from the previous calculation of every five days overdue as one month. The pawnshops could not bear this impact. Special representatives were elected to come to the province and petition the Provincial Government yesterday afternoon. Chairman Ye met with them, and the representatives stated their grievances, requesting that the difficulties of businesses be taken into consideration and that implementation be temporarily suspended. Chairman Ye replied that this matter was of great importance to the poor and it was not appropriate to approve their request and agreed to submit it to the Provincial Government for discussion. The representatives were satisfied and dispersed.

Yangzhou 91

Magistrate Xu Escaped from Office: Xu Zusheng, the magistrate of Yangzhou County, was ordered to be dismissed.

Because of excessive embezzlement in the collection of funds, the local gentry secretly colluded with the guards, preparing to detain him for liquidation. Learning that Mr. Xu had been trying to persuade Mr. Wang and other gentry to intercede for him, but he could not escape, he took advantage of a recent murder case. On the morning of the 3rd, he took his trusted guards and went to the scene in sedan chairs to investigate. He stayed overnight at the District Office, which was very close to the river. The next morning (4th), he quietly went to the Nan碼头 terminal and boarded a ship to leave Yangzhou. By the time the news reached San茆 Town, the people of Yangzhou were unable to pursue him. After the Education Bureau and others heard the news, they presented a special request to the Provincial authorities for a thorough investigation of the grain accounts to clarify the situation, as they found it difficult to claim the education funds lost due to the magistrate's quiet departure. It is said that Mr. Xu was able to escape from Yangzhou this time because he first obtained the understanding of certain gentry, otherwise it would not have been easy for him to board the ship safely at the Nan碼头. It is rumored that the new magistrate Zhao Enju will assume office on the 6th.

Details of the Lianjie Robbery in Ban'er Sha: In Ban'er Sha, Yangzhou County, many homes were robbed by bandits on the night of the 1st, causing great losses. It is learned that on that night, the bandits started from Shang沙头木 Bridge口大新圩 and went to the Lao母字圩 in the lower section, robbing Zhang Yinghua, Du Qiguo, Leng Changyou, Sun Qilong, Zhou Zhihe, Yang Zhengxing, Li Shishou, Chen Shenggao, Yao Xinglong, Miao Shiyi, Ding Changhe, and other 11 families. The losses of clothing and silver dollars were countless. Zhang Yinghua's eight-year-old child was also kidnapped. That night, the bandits also planned to rob the sand. Fortunately, a nearby resident, Gao, sent someone to report to the County Government, which sent a Public Security Team to the sand to fight bravely. The bandits fled in different directions. Xu Tingkun and Bu Laoer, two suspects captured, were both from northern Jiangsu. The County Government is conducting a preliminary trial, but there is no confession yet and the interrogation is ongoing.

Yangzhou 92

The Case of the Junior High School is Turning Downward Rapidly: Bao Han, the principal of Jiangdu County Junior High School, was previously accused by Shi Songyu, Xiong Jiageng, and others of embezzling public funds. The Education Department ordered the County Education Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation. Later, the case files were stolen from the bureau, and the case was finally transferred to the judicial system. The County Prosecutor's Office opened court three times to investigate. During the last time, Bao applied for an obstruction and failed to appear in court, so the court changed the date to the 6th of this month to continue the investigation of accounts. Currently, a senior member of the education community has been appointed to mediate. Bao Han may resign as principal as a condition for an exchange. If there are no legal problems, it may turn downward rapidly.

The Pacification Commissioner Ordered the Clearance of Local Bandits: Baiyang Mountain, at the intersection of Jiangdu and Yizheng, has many bandit dens and the bandits appear and disappear unpredictably. The police teams of the two counties have gone to the area for joint patrols, but the bandits have fled upon hearing of the patrols. After the police teams withdrew, bandit traces reappeared. Now, Pacification Commissioner Zhang has received reports and specially ordered the County Government to clear the area of bandits. Yesterday (4th), County Magistrate Chen ordered the Ninth District Office in charge to comply. It is also heard that the Yizheng County Government has also received the same order.

Districts Handle Communist Surrender: After the pacification of the Communist bandits in Tongyi, the Party and government agencies decided that all districts would handle Communist surrender at the same time, limited to within this month. Two measures were stipulated: (1) Communist suspects in each district who have been released or not released, if they have already taken photos and filled out forms, they should immediately submit the photos and forms for review. Those who have not taken photos and filled out forms should do so within a specified period. (3) Communist criminals who have surrendered in the District Office and have been released, if they do not submit them for review, will still be considered unrepentant.

Five-County Joint Naval and Land Defense Conference: The political and police chiefs and naval police captains of Nantong, Haimen, Qidong, Chongming, and Changshu counties, totaling more than 20 people, attended the joint naval and land defense conference at the Nantong County Government on the afternoon of the 5th. They discussed and decided on measures to defend against bandits on the river and sea and plans to suppress sea bandits. Pinghu 94

The Bandits Tried to Show Off But Fortunately Did Not Succeed: Ten bandits, each holding sharp weapons, arrived in Ran Dian Bridge Town, three miles outside the East Gate of Zhapu, Pinghu, on the night of the 4th, intending to rob the town. They were spotted by nearby villagers who sounded the gong to raise the alarm. One side ordered people to report to the Zhapu Public Security Sub-bureau. The chief of the First Sub-station led more than 20 police officers to pursue and arrest them. When they were about to arrive at the town, they fired their guns to show their power. The bandits fled upon hearing the sound. Furthermore, six bandit boats with 40 bandits arrived in Datong Bridge Town, Luoxiang, Xinjie, at 3 p.m. on the 3rd, intending to rob the town. At that time, there were 36 large salt boats resting in the town. The salt smugglers heard the sound and mistakenly thought it was a bandit suppression force, so they carried guns to resist. After both sides explained, they retreated. The town was spared a major robbery.

Jiaxing 95

Electricity Fee Reduction Conference: The Jiaxing Yongming Electric Light Company charged 27 cents per degree of electricity and 30 cents per month for fire meter loss fees, causing much complaints from various users. The various merchants jointly submitted a request to the County Government, County Party Department, and County Business Association, requesting the company to improve and reduce electricity fees. The County Government convened a meeting of the members of the Business Association and the company's staff at the Construction Bureau on the 5th. Eight user representatives, including Hu Feiqian and Gui Suxiang, attended. County Secretary Gong Jingzhi chaired the discussion. After mediation by Liang Hua of the Construction Bureau, the electricity fee was reduced by 2 cents per degree and the fire meter loss was reduced by 20 cents, starting from February 1 of this year. Both sides reached an agreement, and the representatives signed the minutes of the resolution, and the meeting adjourned.

Rickshaw Pullers Strike in Jiaxing: After the Jiaxing Rickshaw Company organized the trade association the day before yesterday, it began printing and distributing rickshaw licenses to members of the rickshaw puller trade union on the 5th. The license stated that each vehicle must pay a monthly rental of 12 yuan, so the rickshaw pullers expressed their opposition and demanded a return to the old system of paying rent on a daily basis. Therefore, at noon on the 5th, the rickshaws inside and outside the city went on strike. As of the morning of the 6th, the situation had not been resolved and the rickshaws on the streets were still gone.

County Executive Committee Members Have Been Appointed: The Provincial Executive Committee has appointed Zhou Mingsheng, Zhu Zhenfan, and Cao Xianzhang, who were nominated by the Sixth Jiaxing County Congress, as members of the County Executive Committee, and designated Zhou Mingsheng to convene the first meeting.

Hangzhou 96

Suggestions for Revitalizing Zhejiang Tea: Zhejiang tea's transportation and sales to various countries once held an important position. In recent years, the tea industry has fallen behind, even declining to only a few thousand pounds. If measures are not taken quickly to remedy the situation, the consequences will be unimaginable. The giant merchant Sun Haoji has proposed two ways to revitalize Zhejiang tea and remedy the situation, and has suggested them to the Provincial Government: (1) Internally implement reductions in local tariffs, miscellaneous taxes, and business tax rates, and completely exempt export tea taxes, so as to reduce costs and gain a foothold in overseas competition. (2) Establish a tea industry school to cultivate talent, send them abroad to tea-producing areas to conduct detailed inspections, and adopt their strengths to seek various improvements. The Hangjiang Loan Will Be Delivered Soon: For the Hangjiang Railway loan of 3.5 million yuan, the Construction Department has allocated 1.5 million yuan from the construction bonds and the power plant surplus of 500,000 yuan. There is still a shortage of 2 million, which the Shanghai banking community is trying to raise. The Construction Department received a telegram from Shanghai yesterday stating that the loan of 2 million yuan will be paid immediately. There are slight changes in the content of the contract. We will send someone to your department in the next few days to discuss the implementation and sign the agreement.

Compilation of Kidnapping and Robbery Cases: (1) Six or seven bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Ma Fucheng in Shi Gongshan Village, Yuyao, and robbed it extensively, and kidnapped Ma's 14-year-old son, Ma Zhulian. Qingdao 98

The Organization of the Qingdao Municipal Hospital: Since Mayor Hu Ruoyu took over the Qingdao Municipal Government, he has actively reorganized the municipal administration. He noted that the city only has two hospitals, Puj济 Hospital and the Infectious Disease Hospital, as well as the Licun Branch, which belongs to Puj济, and the Inspection Institute, which is dedicated to testing sanitation supplies. Chen Youren Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 100

▲ Came with his wife, Ms. Zhang

Former Foreign Minister Chen Youren arrived in Shanghai at 5 p.m. yesterday on the Japanese ship Zhushan Maru from France. Mr. Chen has been away from the country for three years. Last year, he married Ms. Zhang Jingjiang at the Chinese Embassy in Paris. The wedding was officiated by Gao Lu, the Chinese Ambassador to France. Mrs. Chen also returned to the country together this time. Mr. Chen is well-known in diplomatic circles. In the 16th year of the Republic of China, he had a dispute with British Counselor O'Malley over the British concession in Hankou, which ended in its recovery, opening a new chapter in China's diplomatic history. When our reporter heard that Chen had returned to the country, he went to inquire, but Chen said it was late and would talk another day.

Finance Minister Song's Remarks 103

The reporter from the Guowen News Agency met with Finance Minister Song Ziwen yesterday and asked him about some matters. The replies are recorded as follows: (1) The dumping tax that is being planned is the hoarding tax. It is currently being reviewed and handled by the Ministries of Finance and Industry. (2) The business tax in the concessions should also be implemented at the same time. It is currently being carried out by the Shanghai Municipal Government. Difficulties with Unified Cotton Yarn Tax Resolved Yesterday 104

▲ Tax Forms Handled According to the Wheat Flour Unified Tax

▲ Cloth Tax Collection Method Based on Net Yarn

▲ Tax Payments Cleared Monthly

The Riri News Agency reported that representatives from the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui who represented the Chinese cotton mills petitioned Director Xie of the Unified Tax Department the afternoon before yesterday, stating their difficulties. It was decided that several responsible representatives would be selected by the representatives to discuss and resolve all difficulties at the Unified Tax Department on the Bund of Hankou Road at 9 a.m. yesterday. At 9 a.m. yesterday morning, Xu Qingyun, Guo Shun, Zhang Zemin, Tang Xinghai, Wang Qiyu, Chen Wanyun, Li Shenhou, Nie Lusheng, and other eight representatives from the Chinese cotton mills arrived at the Unified Tax Department on time. Director Xie Zuokai of the Department was very busy with official duties, so Wang Zong, the director of the Unified Tax Bureau of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, Dong Zhongding, the secretary of the Unified Tax Department, Wang Junzhi, the chief of the First Section, Liang Jiagan, the chief of the Fifth Section, and Zhou Jiechun, the chief of the Sixth Section, met with the representatives in the reception room. Both sides discussed together, and the results were: (1) Extending the deadline for clearing the existing inventory. Director Shan Xie asked the Minister of Finance for instructions, and there was no problem after the reply. It was not discussed further. (2) Simplify the tax procedures as much as possible. All unified cotton yarn tax forms will be handled in the same way as the unified wheat flour tax. The previously determined forms No. 11, No. 13, No. 16, and No. 17 will not be used temporarily. (3) When cotton yarn leaves the factory, it will be in units of ten small packages or four small packages per piece. The Unified Tax Bureau will issue a separate transportation bill. Cotton yarn of less than ten small packages will not be inspected for the time being after paying the unified tax. (4) For each piece of cotton yarn, the original standard was 315 jin for those below 23 counts, 310 jin for those above 23 counts, and 300 jin for those above 60 counts to 80 counts. Now, it has been changed to 312 jin for those below 23 counts, and 310 jin for all those above 23 counts. (5) For cloth tax collection, because various factories purchase yarn from other factories and mix it in, and because of the paste on the cloth, it has been decided that for yarn spun by the spinning mills themselves and delivered to the weaving factories, the resident tax collectors will register the yarn quantity and collect the tax according to the net yarn. (6) All taxes will be registered in the accounts by the resident tax collectors. On the 25th of each month, the registered amount will be closed once and the tax will be calculated. Before the 30th of each month, each factory will fully pay the tax. Both sides were satisfied with the above items. The representatives left at 12:30.

British and Japanese Gauze Industries Petitioned the General Taxation Bureau Yesterday 105

▲ British Merchants Petition: Yesterday afternoon, representatives from British-owned Ewo Cotton Mill, Public Cotton Mill, and Yangshupu Cotton Mill, consisting of three British and three Chinese representatives, went to the General Taxation Bureau to petition. They were received by Deputy Director Shi, Section Chief Liang, and Technical Expert Zeng, among others. The representatives raised issues regarding procedures. Subsequently, due to several unclear aspects of the General Taxation Regulations, they reviewed the regulations item by item until 6:00 PM. The original points of request were not brought up.

▲ Japanese Merchants Petition: Since the implementation of the General Taxation Regulations, Japanese-owned gauze mills in this port had initially been observing the situation. However, due to the requests made by Chinese-owned mills to the bureau in recent days, representatives from Japanese-owned Naigai Cotton Mill, Japanese-owned mills Association in China, and others, totaling six individuals, also petitioned the General Taxation Bureau yesterday at 4:00 PM. They were received by Technical Expert Zeng, representing the bureau. The Japanese merchants stated that they did not oppose the General Taxation Regulations. However, since Chinese merchants had already requested reduced procedures, they requested equal treatment for both Chinese and Japanese parties. Technical Expert Zeng explained each point of the Chinese merchants' requests and stated that there would be equal treatment for both Chinese and foreign parties, without any favoritism. The Japanese representatives expressed their satisfaction and departed.

Shanghai City's Handling of the Business Tax Issue 106

▲ Chamber of Commerce Forms a Special Committee

▲ Representatives Designated to Attend the Bureau of Finance

Regarding the handling of the business tax issue in Shanghai, it is reported that the Bureau of Finance has sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting the appointment of representatives to participate in discussions. The Chamber of Commerce has formed a committee to conduct research. The following is a record of various news items:

▲ Municipal Chamber of Commerce Held Executive Committee Meeting Yesterday: Yesterday at 4:00 PM, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held its first executive committee standing meeting. Over twenty people attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Fang Jiaobo, Luo Qinghua, Zhu Wenqi, Lu Fengzhu, Pei Xueqing, Yuan Ludeng, Xu Ji, Wang Yansong, Cheng Xiechun, Wen Lanting, Ma Jiliang, and Chen Songyuan. Chairman Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting, and Secretary Yan E’sheng reported on various documents regarding the business tax issue. The chairman also reported on the efforts made to reduce tax rates during discussions in Zhejiang Province. The following items were then discussed: (1) A proposal from the Standing Committee to form a Business Tax Research Committee. It was noted that the business tax issue had been handled according to the resolutions of the tenth executive committee meeting, and instructions and replies had been received. The implementation of the business tax in Shanghai was reportedly underway, and various industries had sent letters to the chamber requesting a reduction in tax rates. The thirtieth standing committee meeting on the second of this month discussed and agreed that it was necessary to form a special committee to conduct detailed research. A proposal with reasons was submitted to the executive committee for discussion and decision. It was resolved to appoint eleven members, including Chen Songyuan, Luo Qinghua, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Wenqi, Wang Yansong, Lu Qisheng, Ma Jiliang, Shao Baoxing, Cheng Youfu, Zhuang Meitang, and Xiang Songmao, as committee members, with Wang Yansong as the convener. (2) A discussion on a letter from the Municipal Bureau of Finance requesting the designation of one to five representatives. It was resolved to appoint five committee members, including Wang Yansong, Luo Qinghua, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Wenqi, and Chen Songyuan, as representatives.

▲ Suggestions from the Industry Tax Regulations Research Association: The Shanghai Industry Guilds Tax Regulations Research Committee sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, the primary consideration in the collection of business tax is to avoid harming merchants. Therefore, the central government stipulated guidelines for business tax collection, explicitly mandating collection by industry to avoid the trouble of investigations and eliminate the path for extortion. The intention is extremely thorough. However, the draft tax rates proposed by Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces still use goods as the unit and do not follow the method of dividing by industry. For example, Southern goods dealers sell sugar, ginseng, bird's nest, and ham. The North-South goods industry would be taxed at 5 per mille, sugar and ham at 15 per mille, and ginseng and bird's nest at 20 per mille. The categorization is excessively detailed and confusing. In practice, merchants cannot keep accounts by category. As a result, tax collectors will inevitably use the different tax rates as an excuse to inspect accounts and verify inventory, which will inevitably lead to chaos and endless trouble. The means of extortion will begin from here. Furthermore, the tax is called business tax, so it should be collected on the business, not on the category of goods, which would repeat the mistakes of the previous goods likin tax. As for curbing extravagance, it can be handled separately in the special consumption tax. We have read the Regulations for the Collection of Business Tax passed by the Anhui Provincial Government. Article 4 stipulates that all businesses with an annual business income of 1,000 yuan or more shall pay business tax at a rate of 2 per mille. For the preceding ratio, those with 1,000 yuan shall pay 4 yuan, and the remaining amount shall be increased in units of 500 yuan. This seems simple and easy to implement. We earnestly request that your esteemed association telegraph the Ministry of Finance that, unless the government has other regulations below 2 per mille, the tax rate shall not exceed 2 per mille. The wholesale portion should still be taxed at one-quarter of the rate. The collection method should be based on the proportion of business volume as proposed by Anhui Province, in order to avoid harassment and eliminate malpractices. We eagerly await your response." Addressed to: Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

▲ The Ministry-Issued Outline Matches the Original Plan: Yan E’sheng, secretary of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, discussed yesterday's report that the National Business Federation telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating that the business tax outline issued in the Ministry of Finance's telegram No. 5492 differed significantly from the one resolved by the National Economy Conference in July of the 17th year of the Republic. It was found that the matter originated on the 3rd of this month when the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance for clarification, stating that although the outline issued by the ministry also contained nine articles, why did its content differ from the original plan of the Liquidation Conference? In fact, there were no errors in the outline issued by the ministry. The Wuxi Silk Merchants Association based their understanding on the documents of the initial review meeting of the Liquidation Conference. However, at the general meeting on July 21 of that year, it was handed over to the review committee for a second review. The result was a major revision of the original review. At the general meeting on July 24 of that year, the second review report was slightly revised and formally passed. Its content completely matched what the Zhejiang Finance Department was based on this time. In the section on the nature of cases that should be banned, the sentence "or hindering the development of national goods" was removed. Also, in Article 5, the words "review and deliberation" were changed to "evaluation." There were no other major changes. Therefore, the National Business Federation's telegram to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that the outline did not match the original plan, was actually a misunderstanding.

Pan Xulun Replies to the Tax Regulations Research Association 107

▲ Reduce Business Tax Rates

▲ All Chinese People Have Sympathy

The Shanghai Industry Guilds Tax Regulations Research Committee sent a letter to accountants Pan Xulun and Xu Yongzuo, discussing business tax rates. Accountant Xu replied earlier, and the letter was recorded in a previous report. It is now reported that accountant Pan recently went to Beijing to prepare for the National Government's Directorate-General of Budget, and only returned to Shanghai yesterday. He immediately replied to the association. The draft of his letter is recorded below:

"In reply, I recently received your esteemed letter, and I am grateful for your teachings regarding the business tax collection matter. Several accountants recently went to Beijing to prepare for the National Government's Directorate-General of Budget, and only returned yesterday. I apologize for not being able to reply to your letter immediately. I believe that the fact that our country's industries are impoverished and can no longer bear heavy taxes is a universally acknowledged fact. Every time our accounting firm attended meetings on economic, industrial, commercial, financial, and legal regulations, we also made statements to this effect, upholding the purpose of protecting industry and commerce. When we were invited by the Zhejiang Finance Department to participate in the provincial business tax meeting in Hangzhou, we also focused on reducing and equalizing tax rates. I still remember that the draft of the Zhejiang Industry Business Tax Regulations originally stipulated that wholesale merchants should pay half the fixed business tax rate. Several accountants believed that since goods are transferred and sold wholesale many times, half the fixed rate would be too high. They immediately proposed changing it to one-quarter of the fixed rate. Fortunately, the Zhejiang authorities adopted the revised article, and the draft drawn up by Shanghai also uses this point as the basis (the Jiangsu Province draft still uses half the rate and has not been changed). The results of discussions on other tax rate points were also much lower than the originally set numbers. It can be seen that reducing tax rates and promoting industry and commerce is something that all Chinese people have sympathy for, not just your esteemed association. As for the statement in your association's letter that a certain expert compared to foreign tax rates during the Zhejiang meeting, during the sessions attended by our accounting firm, we only heard that a certain gentleman had four calculation standards for business tax collection in foreign countries (i.e., business volume, capital amount, rent amount, and salary amount). We did not hear any expert use foreign tax rates as a comparison. What your association heard may have been a misinterpretation of hearsay. I am writing this letter specifically to reply. I hope you will understand. As for the business tax rate in Shanghai, the municipal authorities have already drafted a plan, but the Financial Discussion Committee has not yet discussed it. If our accounting firm is invited to participate in the discussion, we will contribute our usual opinions to the authorities in the hope that the tax rate will be suitable for the national conditions." Addressed to: Shanghai Industry Guilds Tax Regulations Research Committee.

Foil Industry Guild Requests Reduced Tax Rate 108

▲ Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Foil Industry Guild sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, the Zhejiang Province's business tax rate for foil is set at 15 per mille, which violates the Ministry's regulations. Our guild previously submitted evidence and requested your esteemed association's assistance in forwarding the situation to the Ministry of Finance to request the Zhejiang Provincial Government to return the collected taxes and reduce the tax rate. However, many days have passed, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government has ignored it. Moreover, merchants are being solicited to contract and package goods, and the tax receipts issued are still for business tax, so they cannot be reported to the customs for shipment, hindering sales and causing significant losses. The end of the general settlement period is approaching, and if goods cannot circulate, how can funds be turned over? The industry is running around in panic. The purpose of liquidation was to relieve the pain of merchants and civilians, but what our industry has encountered is the opposite. If this continues, how can the future of the industry be imagined? Therefore, we are submitting this letter to state the situation. We respectfully request that your esteemed association telegraph the Ministry of Finance to immediately abolish the Zhejiang Province's illegal foil business tax bureau, return the collected taxes, and change to a one-item-one-tax system that is implemented nationwide. The new tax rate should not exceed the old tax amount, in order to comply with the resolutions of the Five Provinces Liquidation Conference and fulfill the credibility of the central government, and to reduce the burden and relieve the plight of Jiangsu merchants. We await your urgent instructions." Addressed to: Chairman and Committee Members of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Chen Yongnian.

The Shanghai Candle Industry Guild has been receiving telegrams from industry peers in Beijing, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Yangzhou, Suzhou, Wuxi, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, Shaoxing, and other places, stating that the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial governments recently set business tax rates, taxing the industry's products at 20 per mille, nearly ten times the outline issued by the ministry. The industry's profits are all from handicrafts and labor, and cannot bear this heavy tax. Jiangsu and Zhejiang are closely related, and should jointly present the situation to the Jiangsu and Zhejiang authorities to strive for a reduction, ensuring that it does not exceed the Ministry's fixed standard of 2 per mille. The telegram submitted for record is recorded below: "To the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, Nanjing Municipal Government, Jiangsu Provincial Government, Zhejiang Provincial Government, and Shanghai Municipal Government of the National Government of Nanjing: In accordance with Article 14 of the revised Industrial and Commercial Guild Law, two or more industrial and commercial guilds may form a joint association with the consent of more than one-third of their members. If the joined industrial and commercial guilds belong to the same province, the constitution of the joint association shall be approved by the provincial government and reported to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for record. If they do not belong to the same province, or cross provinces, or are directly subordinate to the Executive Yuan, they shall be approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, etc. Now, after deliberation by representatives of the incense and candle industry guilds of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, and Shanghai, the Joint Association of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, and Shanghai Incense and Candle Industry Guilds has been legally organized. Fifteen people, including He Yinsheng, Li Maosheng, Zhu Yongyuan, Zheng Fangbiao, Sun Yaoxun, Zhang Yuzhen, Xu Ruiqing, Wu Yuebo, Qian Xingqiao, Chen Zhongxin, Gu Xiaoshan, Sun Xianglin, Xu Zijing, Yang Yunxiang, and Shen Genpei, have been provisionally designated as preparatory committee members. The preparatory office is temporarily located at No. 3 Sanyi Lane, Ninghe Road, Nanshi, Shanghai, inside the Shanghai Candle Industry Guild, and will begin work immediately. We will submit the drafted constitution separately for review. In addition to this, we should first telegraph your ministry and government for approval and ask for your permission to put it on record. It will be for the public benefit. Joint Association of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Beijing, and Shanghai Incense and Candle Industry Guilds Preparatory Office (micro-printed)."

Anti-Opium Association Publishes Sun Yat-sen's Anti-Smoking Stance 110

▲ Premier's Teachings as a Compass for the Authorities

Recently, there have been divergent views on anti-smoking measures. Some advocate for public sale, others advocate for disguised public sale, and others advocate for absolute prohibition. The rumors are confusing and there is no consensus. The Chinese National Anti-Opium Association, in order to awaken the attention of compatriots and party and government authorities, and to correct the rumors advocating for public sale, has published the full text of Sun Yat-sen's anti-smoking stance, which he published in Guangzhou in 1924 when he was serving as Grand Marshal, as a standard for those advocating for the prohibition of smoking. At a time of such divergent opinions, the Premier's teachings can truly serve as a compass for the authorities implementing anti-smoking measures. The full text is reproduced below:

"In my opinion, the problem of smoking prohibition in China is related to the problem of good government. The business of opium is absolutely incompatible with a democratic government endowed with power by the people. However, until the government authorities have realized the authority of democracy in the implementation of public administration, effective prohibition is hardly possible. At present, the lawless warlords are not only encouraging but also forcing the planting of opium within their jurisdictions. Elaborate and detailed plans for smoking prohibition are of little use. This is because planting opium is simpler and more profitable than planting rice, grains, vegetables, fruits, and other things. Therefore, farmers are generally unwilling and dare not oppose the warlords' orders to force the planting of opium. The International League of Nations' anti-smoking conference is about to open. The representatives of all countries attending the conference should uphold the spirit of fairness and resolutely establish a strict plan to prohibit the production of opium and its derivatives (such as morphine, heroin, and other poisons) in all countries. The result of the fragmentation of the Chinese government has not only revived the planting of opium but also made foreign trade increasingly stagnant. Chinese and foreign merchants and manufacturers of legitimate goods have suffered huge losses. At present, if the huge amount of money consumed by the smuggling and private sale of opium were used for legitimate trade, it would not only revive the domestic economy but also greatly improve legitimate trade between China and foreign countries. Recently, some have said that since opium has revived in our country today and poisons are everywhere, it would be better to legally allow the business of opium and allow foreign opium to be imported through customs in order to enrich the sources of military funds. Such proposals are absolutely inappropriate. Chinese public opinion, especially the opinion of law-abiding, peaceful, and pure people, is invariably opposed to opium. Anyone who advocates legally allowing the business of opium or showing surrender to the evil forces of opium, even if it is a temporary expedient, is a public enemy of public opinion. The domestic situation today is extremely bad, and the anti-poison movement is facing many difficulties, so the results have been very few. However, the war against opium must absolutely not be compromised or abandoned. If the responsible government agency lowers its flag and ceases fighting against opium for its own private convenience and immediate interests, it is an act of treason, no matter how long or short. In short, any surrender to the harm of opium, in any form, can be said to be a disregard for the conscience of the nation. Even the bandit-like warlords who rely on illegal opium as a source of profit dare not openly admit that opium is a legitimate business. They cannot escape the shame and the conscience-stricken rebuke of theft for their own illegal acts. Our country's interior lacks roads and the construction of various convenient transportation facilities. In addition, there are frequent warlord struggles, which result in an increasing economic burden on farmers. It is impossible for farmers to peacefully cultivate ordinary agricultural products. For example, the Guangdong Provincial Government is extremely opposed to smoking and drugs, but in addition to smuggling from neighboring provinces, there is still opium imported from abroad by sea. Under these circumstances, even a good government like Guangdong Province can hardly eliminate the illegal opium business and formulate a detailed plan to eliminate the root of the scourge. However, due to the large amount of smuggling by land and sea, it is impossible to achieve considerable practical results. From this, we can see that local actions are difficult to achieve results. To achieve the goal of smoking prohibition, the National Government must adopt a nationally consistent plan. Therefore, we should first overthrow the warlords who are more deeply harmful and more harmful, promote the establishment of the National Government, and enable it to realize the authority of democracy. Only then can smoking prohibition be effective. Today, once the scourges that hinder the lives and freedoms of the people are abolished, the power of public opinion will surely be able to achieve the goal of prohibiting opium. At present, the warlords have not been overthrown, and the democratic government has not yet unified the country. The best way to achieve the above-mentioned goal is for anti-poison groups to struggle unremittingly, continue to work on investigation and publicity, so that illegal business has nowhere to hide. Even if it may not be effective for a while, we must never give up the determination to struggle with perseverance and non-compromise, and we must always adhere to a thorough non-surrender policy."

Aircraft Manufacturer Zhu Rongzhang Returns to China 113

▲ Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Zhu Rongzhang, a native of Kaiping, Guangdong, went to the United States at his own expense and entered the Curtiss School of Aviation Engineering in Philadelphia to study. In 1923, he transferred to the Curtiss Aviation School in Chicago. After graduating, he returned to Philadelphia and built an aircraft himself, which was highly praised by Chinese and foreigners. He then went to the Aviation Engineering University in Schenectady, New York, to pursue further studies. After graduating in 1929, he was hired by the Seif Aircraft Factory in Chicago. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the President Fillemore ship of the Dollar Company. After a short rest, he will go to Beijing to meet with the authorities and make contributions.
