Jinan Football Team and Zhenru Basketball Team's Philippine Expedition (7) 161

(By Our Reporter Wenchu, Sent from Manila on January 28)

Football Victory Over All-Stars ▲ Score of 2 to 1 丨 Fifth Battle 丨

▲ Unfair Referee Enrages the Crowd

▲ Almost Leading to a Major Sino-Philippine Disturbance

The brave Jinan football players, who were on a solitary expedition and had won several battles, fought the Philippine All-Star Football Team on January 28 at 4:30 PM. Our army harbored the ambition to conquer all, hoping to secure another victory against this strong enemy and sing a song of triumph. The opposing side wanted to make a final struggle, hoping to leave a mark of honor in the football world. Therefore, this final match was even more intense than the previous ones. No wonder the spectators from both sides surged like a tide.

▲ President of the Chinese Education Association Exhorts the Troops

In order to win this final victory, the overseas Chinese community had high hopes. Therefore, they publicly elected Mr. Lin Xijin, President of the Education Association, to visit and comfort the brave soldiers at the main camp before their departure, and he encouraged them even more, boosting their morale. They drove to the front line in a mighty fashion at 4:00 PM.

▲ Opponent's Strength is Empty Reputation

The players this time were based on those who attended the previous Far Eastern Football Games, and they also selected top players from various schools to join, with many of Spanish descent. Each of them looked mighty, showing 120% fighting ability. Therefore, they were called the Philippine All-Star Team. But when the sun comes out, all the stars dim.

▲ Zhang Wo Valiantly Succeeds in an Instant

When the time came, the whistle blew, and our army faced the sun in formation. The center forward Dai passed the ball and commanded the entire army to take a flanking position, attacking the enemy's goal. Dai dribbled the ball quickly, knowing that the opponent would be prepared for a long shot. Therefore, after dodging the enemy's midfielder, he passed it to Fu Hexuan. Fu dribbled for a few steps and then passed it to Dai. Dai knew that the enemy would be closely monitoring him and that the black general was closely following behind, so he deliberately let the ball go. The black general had already understood the plan and quickly hooked the ball with his left foot. The ball flew into the right corner with great force. Their cooperative spirit was such. Since the few matches, success had never been so quick. The enemy's iron gate, praised as the best in the Philippines, did not dare to raise its head after this strike. Since they were called the All-Star Team, they were naturally not easy to deal with. They did not lose heart due to one failure. The forwards, taking advantage of the kick-off, tried their best to counterattack, but they were all blocked by our brave defenders, General Ma and Jiang Shanqing.

▲ Long-Legged Immortal Displays His Supernatural Powers

Since the enemy's fierce attack was unsuccessful, our side took advantage of their slightly loose formation. The five forwards counterattacked at the same time. Center forward Dai received a pass from Mei and went straight to the center. The enemy goalkeeper kicked it back. Before long, Black General dribbled forward, forcing his way to within ten yards of the goal and shooting. The ball hit an enemy player and bounced out. After struggling for a long time, Shu Tang showed his skill of high kicks and long shots, but the enemy goalkeeper caught it and kicked it out. At this time, our side was besieging the enemy city, and the ball shadows were all aimed at the enemy's goal. Their iron gate was agile and defended effectively, so the fortified city was not captured again. After a while, Center forward Dai received a pass from Luo Haiguang and immediately passed it to Black General. Black General immediately sped up and shot hard, but the enemy goalkeeper dove to catch it. Long-Legged Immortal received the ball from General Ma and shot from over thirty yards. The enemy goalkeeper failed to catch it, and the second city was captured by our army again. Before long, the first half ended, and our army won by a large margin of 2 to 0.

▲ Both Sides Fought Bravely Without Ceasing

After the break, the battle resumed, and our side rose with divine power, hoping to honor Long-Legged Immortal with a chicken egg. Long-Legged Immortal got the ball on the right and tried a long shot again, but unfortunately, he used too much force and the ball went over the goal. The enemy, being in a losing position, also tried their best to counterattack in order to salvage the situation. Therefore, they launched several fierce counterattacks. Fortunately, our side had a solid defense. At this time, the ball was passing back and forth almost without rest. Once, Black General received a pass from Mei Hongbao and shot with force, while Luo Haiguang and Chen Bingxiang also launched surprise attacks. These were our army's last two attacks, but they were not successful. Who knew that disaster would strike ten minutes before the end of the match?

▲ Referee Suspected of Being Unfair

The enemy, fighting for these last ten minutes, had their right winger get the ball, dribble, and go straight in. He kicked it with great force, and the ball went out of bounds on the right corner. When Xie Quanhe went out to pick up the ball, the referee was still ten yards away. The reporter personally saw an enemy player on the ground pointing to the right corner. The referee immediately blew his whistle and also pointed to the right corner. Our coach, Mr. Wu Yanzhang, who was a linesman on the battlefield at the time, held a flag and wore a uniform, and argued briefly. However, he submitted to the referee's decision and was penalized with a corner kick. The crowd was dissatisfied and shouted loudly. During this dispute, the players did not pay much attention, so the ball was kicked in. Our side had no objections. As soon as we picked up the ball to go back to the center, a Spanish man who was close to the field pushed Mr. Wu Yanzhang hard, and our audience was filled with anger.

▲ Mr. Lin Zhuguang Righteously Argues

When Mr. Lin saw that Mr. Wu had been insulted, he thought that the Spanish were bullying our people too much, so he came forward to argue. Yang Shuhui, a member of the Zhuguang basketball team, also came forward to help Mr. Lin. A police officer arrived, and instead of trying to peacefully resolve the situation, he pushed Mr. Lin hard. Yang wanted to argue, but the police officer blew his whistle, and many police officers rushed over, threatening to arrest people. At that time, the crowd was filled with anger and shouted "Fight!" Some people threw chairs high in the air. The order in the field was chaotic. Because a firecracker was set off at the carnival, women and children became even more frightened. Because the crowd was not under control, one person's recklessness would lead to a collapse like a flood. Therefore, the police arrested any Chinese they saw, and the Chinese beat any Filipinos they saw. Athlete Lin Songfa originally wanted to mediate, but the police also wanted to arrest him. Chen Zhang'e wanted to explain and was also about to be arrested. Overseas Chinese businessman Li Fengrui quickly told the police that if there was any problem, he was willing to go to the police headquarters with Mr. Chen and would not escape. On the one hand, conscious overseas Chinese jointly maintained order. A storm was calmed down in an instant.

▲ Major Negotiations at the Police Station

The police arrested eight Chinese and one Filipino and sent them to the headquarters. At this time, Lin Zhuguang, Zheng Yong'an, and reporters from various newspapers, dozens of people in total, arrived at the police station. Consul General Kuang also rushed to the scene after hearing the news. He personally met with the police chief and asked him to release both sides of the detainees to avoid further escalating the conflict. The police chief declined, saying that one police officer had been injured and that the police officers had many complaints about the overseas Chinese. He said that he wanted to hand the case over to the court for resolution. At this time, lawyer Yang Xigao (a prominent member of the city council), a student of the overseas Chinese, responded to Lin Zhuguang's request and, in his capacity as a lawyer, guaranteed the release of the detainees. Liu Qinggao, the consul general of the charity association (also a student of the overseas Chinese), also tried his best to mediate. By the morning of the 29th, charges against six people were dropped, but two people had to await court resolution.

A: Mr. G, after arriving in Shanghai, fell into a love trap.

B: That's not surprising. Shanghai is not like other places. It's a place of romance and beauty.

A: The most shocking thing is that he fell in love with six women at the same time. The golden arrows in the hands of the god of love are too busy.

A Record of Enlightenment Regarding the Fire on Gongjia Road 163

Mr. Chen Yalou of my hometown, practiced medicine during his lifetime. In his medical practice, regardless of rich or poor, near or far, he was not meticulous about the amount of consultation fees. If it was a family in abject poverty, even if it was an external ailment, he would not accept consultation fees or medicine costs. If it was an internal ailment, he would sometimes even provide funds for the family to purchase medicine and coal for boiling it. After prescribing the medicine, he would instead give them money to buy medicine and coal. Or, if he saw a family without mats in the summer or blankets in the winter, he would give them money to buy mats and blankets. Such was his lifelong medical practice. Therefore, during one serious illness, he had died for several hours. The family had already prepared clothing, bedding, and a coffin, but Mr. Chen suddenly revived. From then on, he did even more good deeds. In his later years, in addition to providing free consultations and medicine, he also repaired bridges and roads in the surrounding villages. He realized that one person's strength was limited, so he gathered twelve gentlemen and merchants in the village to establish the "Tongshan Benevolent Society." Each member of the society would contribute funds annually to build a stone bridge, with the goal of building twelve stone bridges within twelve years to benefit travel in the surrounding villages. Unfortunately, before the work was even half completed, Mr. Chen suddenly passed away, unable to see its success. Mr. Chen only possessed a modest amount of property, but whenever there were floods or droughts in various places, he would not hesitate to donate generously to relief efforts. He was so fond of doing good deeds. This is truly rare and commendable. In the Xinhai year of the Xuantong era, Mr. Chen and a Mr. Lu jointly purchased a house belonging to a certain family on Gongjia Road. In the first year of the Republic of China, they moved to Gongjia Road. The house faced the town in the front and bordered the river in the back, with two main halls in the front and back, and wing rooms on the left and right. Mr. Chen lived in the right wing room, while the left wing room was rented out by Mr. Lu. The left wing room belonged to Mr. Lu, and the right wing room belonged to Mr. Chen. The front and back halls were jointly owned by both families. After Mr. Chen passed away two years ago, his family did not bury him. His coffin was placed in the back hall. On the evening of the 25th of last month, Mr. Wan, a tenant in Mr. Lu's room, was careless with fire, and a fire broke out in the left wing room, erupting through the roof. The fire was spreading rapidly. When the fire started, the wind was blowing directly towards the back hall. The front hall was completely engulfed in flames, and the back hall bordered the river, making it impossible to move the coffin. Just as the family was in a state of panic, the back hall also caught fire. They were left to let it happen naturally. Who knew that when the fire reached the back hall, the wind, which had been blowing southwest, suddenly changed direction to southeast, swirling around. The fire was extinguished. Upon inspection afterward, Mr. Lu's left wing room was completely destroyed, while the front and back halls only had a few rafters burned, forming a narrow alley. Mr. Chen's property and coffin were not damaged. Some say this was due to Mr. Chen's lifelong good deeds. The Buddhist saying of cause and effect is indeed believable.

### Three-Hundred-Year-Old Ancient Cannon Unearthed Chen Xianrong 164

Beiping was the former imperial capital of past emperors. Its historical sites and artifacts are enough to evoke a sense of nostalgia for the past. The most notable is the recent excavation of a 300-year-old ancient cannon. This ancient cannon was buried in the ground. This time, the Ping Municipal Works Bureau started construction to build roads and discovered it. A total of seventy cannons were found. The cannons were engraved with the names of Wu Sangui, Chen Guodong, etc. The antique color is mottled, which is indeed an old object from 300 years ago and is extremely precious. It is heard that after the ancient cannons were unearthed, the municipal government has displayed it at the Relics Preservation Office, so that people can visit and appreciate for evaluation and preservation.

Fuzhou Hot Springs Jia Qing 165

The Huaqing Hot Springs, where the emperor granted bathing in the spring cold, has been passed down as a beautiful story for thousands of years. And Nanjing's Tangshan, since the capital was established, has become famous because party and state officials often took their vacations here. Only the hot springs of Fuzhou are rarely known. I have traveled in Fujian for two years and often go to bathe there. I will record it in the Free Talk.

The northeast gate of the Fujian city wall is called Tangmen, named after Tangquan (hot spring). The spring lies dormant in the ground. Along Tangmen, bathhouses are lined up. They all dig wells to extract the spring. The spring gushes out like boiling water, with steaming vapor, like the steam above a pot. A winch is installed on the well, and the liquid is led into the pipe, and then into each room. The water is very hot and needs to be mixed with cold water for bathing. As for the bathrooms in the Wangzhuang Nantai area in the south of the city, the pipes are buried in the ground as underground channels to guide the water. It is estimated that it can be about five miles, and the spring is still warm. However, the installation cost is quite high.

The system of the pool is also very different from that of Shanghai. It is divided into general pool, personal pool, and special pool. There are about 20 personal pools, which are tiled with ceramic tiles. It is wide and suitable for one person to bathe in. It is about two feet deep. Inject the hot spring to fill it, and one end is built like a pillow. When bathing, lie down in the spring, floating up and down, which is very comfortable. The spring is a natural hot spring, so the supply is not stingy. It is more comfortable than the so-called official basins and foreign basins in Shanghai. The general pool is quite large, and many people bathe together. The cost is very cheap. Each person only needs more than ten copper coins. Therefore, many people in the middle and lower classes bathe here.

The most beautiful bathhouse is Letian Spring in Wangzhuang. The special pool is especially elegant. Gentry, businessmen, and figures in institutions all bathe here. There are also barber shops and restaurants. Therefore, welcoming guests from afar and secret negotiations for litigation and mediation are often held in the bathhouse. As for lying on a couch in the hot summer, not knowing dusk, and using the bathhouse as a place to cool off, it is even more common. There is also a Naval United Club in Wangzhuang, which is specially set up for military and political figures. Chairman Yang Shuzhuang and naval figure Chen Jiliang often host guests and celebrate here.

Last summer, a certain family in Tangmen set up a female bathhouse. All the staff were female maids. The content is not known in detail. However, major bathhouses such as Letianquan have also added female seats as a result. A part of the bathroom is marked with a female bathroom, and we cannot cross the forbidden area.

Glass House Guo Xin 166

Pierre Blouke, a famous American architect, has recently invented a glass house. Trees, benches, chairs, tables, everything is available, and all are made of glass. This house can be disassembled and carried like a car. According to Mr. White, this glass house will be popular in the world in less than three years. The house moves with people, and home is everywhere. The suffering of relocation can be greatly reduced. The house is entirely made of glass. The inside and outside of the walls are made of thick glass, leaving a vacuum in the middle, so that cold and heat cannot invade. Those who live indoors always feel warm and have the joy of warmth and harmony, without the suffering of severe winter and severe summer. All the equipment is attached to the house. All the needs of daily life, food and drink are fully available. There are also two ready-made typewriters to replace the labor of holding a pen. This house can be disassembled and packed into a crate for carrying back and forth. When you want to use it, you only need to hire a craftsman to assemble it and you can live in it.

Paris Tales (256) Once Lived in Paris 167

This national arena was probably built in the second century or the beginning of the third century. Many ancient books have already mentioned it. But it was not accidentally discovered until 1870, and was not fully excavated until 1883. We can imagine that this is a symbol of Roman civilization just by looking at these smooth stone blocks inlaid row by row with solid cement. Because the Gaul people living in Paris at that time only had wooden buildings. The architectural design of this arena is very complete. The stone steps can seat 16,000 spectators. There are devices for guiding rainwater in the arena, and devices for holding wild animals, etc. The design is so thoughtful that even the minds of the 20th century cannot match it. At that time, the performances held on this open-air stage included gladiatorial combat and hunting, animal shows and various small tricks popular on the streets, and simple popular dramas. When we walk into this arena, we can imagine the residents of Lutece sitting in rows on these stone steps during festivals, applauding and cheering for the swordsmen or actors of the time. Although the street outside twenty steps away is thundering like thunder with trams and cars, we can sit on the stone seats of this ancient theater and dream for a thousand years. Living in modern life and yearning for the culture of the past. I am afraid that only the residents of Paris can easily get this kind of leisure.

Now, part of the upper flat ground of this ancient arena has been converted into a small park. The arrangement is appropriate, which can reduce the desolate taste common to ancient sites. The outside of the small garden is surrounded by five- or six-story residential buildings. This makes it feel like the modern society and the remains of past life are blended together. Ordinary people don't pay much attention to these places. So it is very difficult to truly understand Paris.

Its convenience is really beyond imagination. Mr. Harvey Wiley Corbett, the current chairman of the Chicago Board of Agriculture, has asked Mr. Bai to manufacture a glass house for him to give to his wife. It will probably be completed next year. Mr. Bai told people that in less than ten years, people all over the world will use this glass house. Therefore, large-scale housing manufacturing plants will be established in various central locations in the United States in the future, specializing in manufacturing various glass residences. After they are manufactured, they will be transported to various places for sale, just like today's cars.

Snippets from Newspaper Reading Chicken Crown 168

Newspapers are a daily necessity. Since residing in the capital, I can only receive the Shen and Xin newspapers from Shanghai in the afternoon after 5:00 PM at the earliest. As for local newspapers, because the land area is vast and delivery takes time, they usually arrive around 11:00 AM. If living in Xiaguan, it will be slightly later. Compared with the residents of Shanghai's northern and southern cities, who can hold newspapers and browse them every morning, I cannot help but feel regretful. Shanghai's tabloids are emerging like a rising tide, but in the capital, the situation is very different. Apart from one or two types, I have not been able to see the rest. On the Beijing-Shanghai trains, tabloids are sold in sets, priced particularly high, and they refuse to separate them. Guests coming from Shanghai usually do not mind the price, using them to dispel boredom. However, when the train arrives in Xiaguan, they often discard them to avoid inspection by the station staff, who will confiscate them if seen. These left-over tabloids are collected and sorted by the train vendors and can still be resold for a second time. It cannot be said that this is not a good business.

In the capital, subscribing to various newspapers from Shanghai from newspaper vendors generally costs one gold yuan per month. There is also a flexible arrangement, that is, the newspaper is delivered on the day and returned by the vendor the next day. In this way, the cost can be reduced to half the price. Also, at the end of the month, all the old newspapers are bundled up. If there are no missing issues, the newspaper price can also be discounted. This is because the waste newspapers are sold by the vendors, and the result is still profitable.

My neighbor has a Miss Lu, who works as a staff member in a certain department. According to her, in addition to copying, she is also busy cutting newspapers every day. Various daily newspapers are prepared on her desk. She first reads them carefully, selects important and relevant news, cuts them out piece by piece, and pastes them on white paper, presenting them to her superiors every day for reference. This is probably because the superiors are too busy with official duties and have no time to read everything, so they have to go through the procedure of a female staff member. But the selection process takes a lot of effort, and the scissors and paste are also very similar to a reporter's life.

▲Acknowledgement and Introduction: Maceol Dental Clinic has hundreds of bottles of French tooth washing liquid. Each bottle was originally worth three taels and two cents of Chinese currency and can wash teeth fifty times. Each time, the cleaning fee is three yuan. Now, due to important matters, he is returning to his country, so he is selling at a loss. Each yuan can get two bottles. Add one yuan for postage outside of Shanghai. The Shanghai Sima Road No. 512 newspaper office, Sanma Road Guangxi Road west end, and Minsheng Hospital all have consignment sales. I received two bottles yesterday, so I would like to express my gratitude and introduce them.

Chapter 17: Ways to Preserve Youth, Green Eyebrows Mixed with Moth Brows, No Way to Extend Life, Golden Market for Fine Bones

So the old A-Xiu and others told Hua Yuanchun, and said, Sixth Miss, don't get angry. Your luck has not been good these past two years. Half of it is because Shanghai's expenses are too high. Calculating, your business is not too bad, but you can't accumulate money. Every season, you are in deficit. Hua Yuanchun knew that old A-Xiu was here to nag again. She had heard these words more than once. But since she had borrowed their money, there was no way. She had to endure their nagging and also say nice things to them. So she said, Aunt A-Xiu, I understand without you saying it. You have always taken care of me. But don't I, Lao Liu, have a good day? These few dollars of yours, I can't get it out this season. Next season, I will definitely find a way. To be honest, we ladies rely on our bodies. Selling our bodies to pay off debts will not leave you short of a penny. This time, Master Zhang wanted to marry me. He asked me, Lao Liu, how much debt do you owe? I said I owed seven thousand. But I didn't really owe seven thousand. You know that. Because Master Zhang is already over fifty and has three concubines at home, I don't want to marry him. But if I really wanted to marry him, seven thousand wouldn't be a big deal. Don't worry. A-Xiu said, What do I have to worry about? But if a person stays in one place for too long, they will get tired of it. I heard that business in Beijing is very good now. There are many people from the south who go to Beijing to become officials. There are also a group of congressmen. I heard that people from all provinces are there. They are preparing to bring some money to Beijing to spend. Seventh Miss went hunting once and is said to be waiting for several thousand dollars. Plus, she bought a lot of fur coats. One game can draw two or three thousand. They don't rely on calling bureaus to drink, but on these officials gambling. Now, A-Jin, the big-bellied man from Qingyutang, has come to Shanghai to pick up ladies. He asked me if there are any beautiful and outstanding ladies that I can introduce to him. First, the face must be pretty. Second, the person must be lively and good at socializing. Those rigid ladies who look like they "owe you rice and are paying you back with Xian rice" when they see guests are not popular in Beijing. Like you, Sixth Miss, your face is good and your skills are good. When you are happy to socialize with guests, you are really outstanding. If you go to Beijing, I think you will be a first-class girl. Take advantage of your youth and make some money. Sixth Miss, if you are interested, now that big-bellied A-Jin is still picking up ladies, let's contact him first. If A-Jin hears that you, Sixth Miss, are willing to go, I think it will definitely be successful. If it is successful, you can pay me back two-thirds or half of our silver dollars first. The rest, I will consider it a share. You don't have to stay in Beijing for too long. When you have enough money, be clear-headed and find a good person to marry in the south.

Yarn and Cotton: The Yarn Market Remains in Terror 176

▲ The exchange again increases cash deposit 6 taels

The yarn market fluctuated between morning declines and afternoon gains, with an erratic trend and a dangerous situation. This was mainly due to the strong exchange rate and rising prices of American and Indian cotton, leading to a surge in the exchange market. At the same time, rumors circulated in the market that two major brokerage firms had a large number of short positions in yarn and cotton, and due to the continuous surge in prices, there was talk of them wavering. As a result, buyers believed that a good opportunity had arrived, and buying sentiment became increasingly intense. Honest traders did not dare to move lightly. However, the fluctuations were enormous, with sudden rises and falls of about one to two taels. To avoid danger, the exchange increased the cash deposit for both buyers and sellers by six taels. Currently, the yarn market remains in a sea of ​​storms.

Grain: Ke Xian Rice Inventory About 40,000 Bags 179

▲ Recent Arrivals and Sales Both Slow

Yesterday's Ke Xian rice market condition was quiet again. Guangzhou and Ningbo merchants were watching and not buying. Only Shao merchants bought more than 200 Nanjing brown rice at a price of 8 yuan 4 jiao 2 fen to 8 yuan 3 jiao 3 fen. The inventory of Ke Xian rice in Shanghai is not much. As of yesterday, there were about 40,000 bags, with Jiangxi rice accounting for more than half.

Flour Market Surges with Gold Prices 180

Yesterday, the flour market suddenly showed a sharp rise. Although the quotation for foreign wheat fluctuated slightly, since the surge in gold prices, goods related to international markets have jumped. The nature of the flour market, due to the presence of foreign flour, is inevitably driven by it. Recently, the sellers in the foreign firms have also been silent. Although various factories have made large sales and successively taken profits, the general outside market, in view of the rise in various goods, is also actively buying futures flour. Buyers are also increasingly buying at lower future prices, especially merchants from Nanyang and Yingkou. Although factory sales continued in the middle, the market sentiment was very strong and could not suppress the arrogance of foreign firms. As a result, the prices for the current month and March rose by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, April rose by 2 fen, May rose by 2 fen 2 li and a half, June rose by 2 fen 7 li and a half, and July rose by 3 fen 7 li and a half.

Wheat Market Opens High and Continues to Rise 181

Yesterday's wheat futures also showed a firm upward trend. Merchants from various mainland regions believed that since the standard has reached this level, even if it falls again, it seems to have a limit. Therefore, buyers were very bold. Also, due to customary reasons, the market will soon close. A few shorts were very strong in covering, and several parties were focused on one place, resulting in a very good sentiment, opening high and continuing to rise, especially for distant futures. Observing the future, if there is no impact from foreign wheat, it may be even better. As a result, the price for the current month rose by 4 fen compared to the previous day, March rose by 5 fen, April rose by 6 fen, May rose by 7 fen, June rose by 9 fen, and July rose by 5 fen.

Recent Italian Literary Circles, Saviotti, and the "Return to Tradition" Movement by Wang Tiran 189

Italy has always been a country with the most literary schools and "isms." Some new "isms" in modern literature almost all originated in Italy. However, they arise quickly and disappear quickly. Therefore, the ebb and flow of Italian literary trends is truly a spectacle of unpredictable change. In recent years, because the new trends have been numerous and chaotic, everyone has felt a lack of interest in "new" things. As a result, a reaction has gradually arisen. This reaction is a "return to tradition" movement, a "new" trend that rejects new things and demands old rules and traditions. In modern literature, this trend is, of course, "new," even though it returns to the old and traditional. In the recent manifestations of Western literature, this trend can be clearly seen and has a somewhat universal nature. In America, it is the so-called "Humanism," which opposes science and all new ideas, and calls for a return to the classics and tradition. In England, it is the novelists' "return to tradition" school of novelists, such as Hugh Walpole and J.B. Priestley, who are continuing the tradition of the English novel, inheriting the spirit of the Victorian era in technique and rules, and inheriting the techniques of Dickens in subject matter and content. The most popular works that dominate the English literary scene today are those of this school. In addition, in Italy, there is the aforementioned "return to tradition" movement. This movement has already become increasingly powerful in the current Italian literary scene, with a tendency to dominate everything. In the field of novels, it has promoted a tendency to return to "classicism." In the field of criticism, it has established the center of emerging Italian criticism. Therefore, it can be predicted that this "return to tradition" movement, which contains reactionary overtones and demands rules and harmony, will change the landscape of modern Italian literature. Moreover, from the perspective of the times, this reaction is also an inevitable phenomenon. After the European War, Italy, thanks to Mussolini's administration, actually achieved a temporary state of well-being from a state of instability and exhaustion. The lives of some of the people have, of course, become more stable from being unstable. This kind of stable situation produces a psychology of indulging in comfort and being conservative. As a result, some people reject the new pursuits and new efforts of freely creating by abandoning tradition and breaking away from rules in all social activities, even literature and art, and demand facilities or activities that return to tradition, abide by rules, and are based on convention and conservatism. Therefore, in literary expression, new things are created independently by breaking away from tradition. The weakness of the foundation and the emptiness of the substance could previously cater to the psychology of most people who were wandering, groping, and seeking new paths, but now they can no longer cater to the psychology of most people who dislike change and crave stability. This kind of mood, expressed in literature and art, is the recent reaction in the Italian critical scene that can be called a return to tradition movement.

The center of this movement is the emerging Italian critic Gino Saviotti. Saviotti is a newly emerging general star in the current Italian literary scene. According to current speculation, this star will inevitably have a great relationship with the future fate of Italian literature.

Saviotti is a writer from Genoa. Genoa has never been known for literature and art, but since Saviotti, it is quite possible that it will become the center of Italian literature and art. Milan, Florence, and Rome may not be able to compare with it. The situation is as follows: Last spring, Saviotti founded his organ magazine "Indice" in Genoa. After the magazine was published, Genoa gradually became a new center of attention in the literary and art world. Now, Saviotti's influence has spread throughout Italy and is gradually increasing in importance.

Saviotti was originally a writer with some fame. His articles are often published in some famous Italian magazines or reviews. However, more than a year ago, he felt that the state of the Italian literary and art world was too bad and that something must be wrong. So he carefully investigated and studied it. As a result, his conclusion was that Italian national literature was infected with the disease of grayness of thought. Therefore, he came to prescribe the right medicine. He first wrote down his feelings about this matter and printed them into a fourteen-page booklet entitled "An Overview of Contemporary Literature, Art, and Criticism." This declaration and the articles he published in the first few issues of "Indice" were like his outline of doctrine. His declaration begins like this:

The most common characteristic of contemporary art is "Cerebralismo." This is often the case in those times that are poor in imagination and rich in thought. Painters, sculptors, poets, and novelists, because they are often in contact with foreign literature and art, are more aware of the requirements of art than before. They are wandering between the new and the old. They cling to every breeze, as long as it carries the hope of clearing the air, for fear of being too late. Therefore, they are too indifferent to practice. They do not paint, sculpt, or write, but only use colors, stone, words, etc. to create some theories (but to put it more precisely, only some arguments). They are only seeking everything new and original, but they have forgotten that true originality lies in the production of true art.

This conceptualism and love of novelty are the characteristics of all decadent periods... We can see the signs of this situation: formal skills dominate content, just as gorgeous clothes cover the ugliness of a tuberculous body. There are people, but no humanity; there is only a brain, but no heart.

This passage can be said to be Saviotti's main text. Below, he will do his best to elaborate on this meaning. But we must know that he is not a pessimist. He does not think that Italian literature is incurable. He believes that the reform of Italian literature is not only indispensable, but also imminent.

In addition to praising the inevitability of the reform of Italian literature, Saviotti then made a thorough analysis of Italian literature in the past and present, and extended his theory to the theater, painting, sculpture, and poetry. In addition, he also criticized the critics. At the end, his declared proposition is "return to tradition," but it is neither neo-classicism, nor neo-romanticism, nor neo-verisimilitude. His proposition is to have writers continue the tradition of Italian literature, and to learn from classical writers such as Homer, Virgil, and Dante; romantic writers such as Manzoni and Leopordi; and Goldoni and Vergo.

But, in the final analysis, what does this proposition of his mean? His meaning is to return art to art, to make art return to the eternal source of literary and artistic creation. In short, it is that he reaffirms that simple great truth: to produce art, there must be artists.

Saviotti is dissatisfied with the critics of his time. He believes that they are unable to practice their work of examining works of art and guiding young writers. They pay too much attention to writing a "good article" (for future inclusion in the complete works). Their criticism is too impressionistic.

The above is the main point of Saviotti's entire proposition. His publication is run according to these points. Saviotti himself is the editor and critic of this publication. He has clear thoughts and speaks powerfully. In some respects, he has a kind of steady insight of the common people into literary and artistic matters. Appearing in the current Italy, he cannot but become a very extraordinary figure.

Elfer Art Monthly 190

▲Publication Announcement

Elfer Art Monthly is a new organization in the domestic art world. Recently, the society intends to gather the strength of the national art world to carry out a large-scale art movement. It has specially compiled and published a kind of Elfer Art Monthly. The content focuses on art reviews and introductions, especially rich in illustrations of famous works. The writers are all backbone members of the contemporary art scene. It is edited by Chen Zhifo and Ni Yide, and Guo Guni is responsible for printing and distribution. It is reported that the first issue of the inaugural issue is scheduled to be published on February 15, and will be sold by major bookstores.

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introductions

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction, but boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.
